      "body": "A message is getting sent to pending state even after it is already sent to the same user. \n\n**Describe the bug**\nAlready sent messages are sent repeatedly (up to every 5 minutes, for up to 7 days) when a document has two scheduled_tasks with the same due date and one of them is stuck in scheduled state. This was seen in some of the instances randomly. Now, the issue has been occuring more frequently causing CHT to send up to 1900 SMS messages over period of 7 days. \n\nThis means a single patient can receive the same SMS message up to ~2,016 times (7 days × 24 hours × 60 min / 5 min) in the worst case.\n\n**Expected behavior**\nOnce the task is processed, it should no longer be sent to pending queue regardless of the state of other tasks. Process tasks in current window that are only in `scheduled` state. \n\n**Environment**\n- Instance: All\n- Browser: Any\n- Client platform: Any\n- App: webapp, sentinel\n- Version: 4.22.0, 5.1.0, known to have existed on all 3.x versions as well\n\n**Additional context*\nI've posted detail on this in medic/config-lumbini/issues/221 (private repo).",

      "body": "# Planning - CHT Community \n\n- [x] Create an GH Milestone for the release and add this issue to it.\n- [x] Add all the issues to be worked on to the Milestone.\n- [x] Ensure that all issues are labelled correctly, particularly ensure that \"Regressions\" are labelled with \"Affects: <version>\" labels. The \"Affects\" label is used in a link in the Known Issues section of the release notes of that version so it has to match exactly. To make sure the label is correct go to the [release notes](https://docs.communityhealthtoolkit.org/core/releases/#release-notes) and ensure the issue is listed.\n\n# Development - Release Manager\n\nWhen development is ready to begin one of the maintainers should be nominated as a Release Manager. They will be responsible for making sure the following tasks are completed though not necessarily completing them.\n\n- [x] Set the version number in `package.json` and `package-lock.json` and submit a PR to the release branch. The easiest way to do this is to use `npm --no-git-tag-version version patch`.\n- [x] Ensure that issues from merged commits are closed and mapped to a milestone.\n- [x] Write an update in the #stewardship-team Slack channel summarising development and identifying any blockers (the [milestone-status](https://github.com/medic/support-scripts/tree/master/milestone-status) script can be used to get a breakdown of the issues). The Release Manager is to update this every week until the version is released.\n\n# Releasing - Release Manager\n\nOnce all issues have been merged into `master` then the release process can start:\n\n- [x] Build a beta named `<major>.<minor>.<patch>-beta.1` by creating a lightweight git tag (e.g. `git tag <major>.<minor>.<patch>-beta.1`) and then push it (e.g. `git push origin tag  <major>.<minor>.<patch>-beta.1`).\n- [x] Once the CI completes successfully and images are built, notify the community by creating a post titled `<major>.<minor>.<patch> Beta Releases` in the [development](https://forum.communityhealthtoolkit.org/c/development/7) category of the CHT forum using this [template](https://forum.communityhealthtoolkit.org/new-topic?title=%3Cmajor%3E.%3Cminor%3E.%3Cpatch%3E%20Beta%20Releases&body=Hi%20Everyone%0AI%E2%80%99ve%20just%20created%20the%20%60%3Cmajor%3E.%3Cminor%3E.%3Cpatch%3E-beta.1%60%20tag.%0APlease%20let%20me%20know%20if%20there%E2%80%99s%20any%20final%20update%20we%20need%20to%20make.%0AIf%20all%20is%20good%2C%20then%20in%2024h%2C%20I%20will%20start%20the%20release.%20Thanks%21&category=development).\n- [x] Go to the [scalability action](https://github.com/medic/cht-core/actions/workflows/scalability.yml) and on the top right, click into \"Run workflow\".  Under \"Use workflow from\" first choose \"tags\" then select the `<major>.<minor>.<minor>-beta.1` tag created above. Then \"Run workflow\". Once it passes, check for the scalability results [here](https://github.com/medic/scalability-results/tree/main/results). More info in the  [scalability documentation](https://github.com/medic/cht-core/blob/master/tests/scalability/README.md).\n- [x] Add release notes to the [Core Framework Releases](https://docs.communityhealthtoolkit.org/core/releases/) page:\n  - [x] Create a new document for the release in the [releases folder](https://github.com/medic/cht-docs/tree/main/content/en/core/releases).\n  - [x] Ensure all issues are in the GH Milestone, they have human readable descriptions, and that they're correctly labelled. In particular: they have one \"Type\" label, \"UI/UX\" if they change the UI, and \"Breaking change\" if appropriate.\n  - [x] Use [this script](https://github.com/medic/cht-core/blob/master/scripts/release-notes/index.js) to export the issues into our release note format.\n  - [x] Collect known migration steps, descriptions, screenshots, videos, data, and anything else to help communicate particularly important changes. This information should already be on the issue, but if not, prompt the change author to provide it.\n  - [x] Document any required or recommended upgrades to our other products (eg: cht-conf, cht-gateway, cht-android).\n  - [x] Ensure that the release notes PR is merged before moving to next step.\n- [x] Create a [new release](https://github.com/medic/cht-core/releases/new) in GitHub, with the naming convention `<major>.<minor>.<patch>`, from the release branch created above as the target branch. Click on the \"Choose a tag\" dropdown and create a tag for the release with the naming convention `<major>.<minor>.<patch>`. Add a link to the release notes page in the description of the release.\n- [ ] Once you publish the release, confirm the release build completes successfully and the new release is available on the [market](https://staging.dev.medicmobile.org/_couch/builds_4/_design/builds/_view/releases). Make sure that the document has new entry with `id: medic:medic:<major>.<minor>.<patch>`\n- [ ] Upgrade the [demo](https://demo-cht.dev.medicmobile.org/) instance to the newly released version.\n  - [ ] From the \"App Management\" admin console (`medic` user creds in 1Password), go to \"Upgrades\" and stage the upgrade for this version.\n  - [ ] Clone `cht-core` repo and checkout the target tag (`git checkout <major>.<minor>.x` ) to ensure you have the proper version of the helm charts.\n  - [ ] In your terminal, change to the `./cht-core/scripts/build/helm` directory.\n  - [ ] Make sure you're using the dev EKS cluster: `kubectl config use-context arn:aws:eks:eu-west-2:720541322708:cluster/dev-cht-eks`\n  - [ ] Ensure you have access to [EKS](https://docs.communityhealthtoolkit.org/hosting/medic/) and  to the [`demo-cht` namespace](https://github.com/medic/medic-infrastructure/issues/1344).) by calling this helm command. There should be no errors: `helm list -n demo-cht`\n  - [ ] Download the current `values.yaml` data from the demo instance: `helm get values demo-cht --namespace demo-cht > values.yaml`\n  - [ ] Edit the `values.yaml` file so `cht_image_tag` and `chtversion` properties have the new tag value `<major>.<minor>.<patch>`.\n  - [ ] Use helm to upgrade the instance: `helm upgrade demo-cht . --namespace demo-cht -f values.yaml`\n  - [ ] Refresh the \"App Management\" page and verify the instance upgraded. You may need to wait 5+ minutes until the upgrade succeeds.  Until then, you may see `50x` errors in the browser - be patient!\n- [ ] Announce the release on the [CHT Forum](https://forum.communityhealthtoolkit.org/), under the \"Announcements - Releases\" category using this [template](https://forum.communityhealthtoolkit.org/new-topic?title=Announcing%20the%20release%20of%20%3Cmajor%3E.%3Cminor%3E.%3Cpatch%3E%20of%20the%20CHT%20Core%20Framework&body=%2AAnnouncing%20the%20release%20of%20%7B%7Bversion%7D%7D%20of%20%7B%7Bproduct%7D%7D%2A%0AThis%20release%20fixes%20%7B%7Bnumber%20of%20bugs%7D%7D.%20Read%20the%20%5Brelease%20notes%5D%28%7B%7Burl%7D%7D%29%20for%20full%20details.&category=releases).\n- [ ] Go over the list of commits and individually notify contributing / interested community members about the release.\n- [ ] Go to the [Issues tab](https://github.com/medic/cht-core/issues) and filter the issues with `is:issue label:\"Affects: 4.x.x\" ` , replace `4.x.x` with the previous version number. Add any open \"known issues\" from the prior release that were not fixed in this release. Done by adding the correct `Affects: 4.x.x` label.\n- [ ] Mark this issue \"done\" and close the Milestone.\n",

Make sure that the document has new entry with `id: medic:medic:<major>.<minor>.<patch>`\n- [ ] Upgrade the [demo](https://demo-cht.dev.medicmobile.org/) instance to the newly released version.\n  - [ ] From the \"App Management\" admin console (`medic` user creds in 1Password), go to \"Upgrades\" and stage the upgrade for this version.\n  - [ ] Clone `cht-core` repo and checkout the target tag (`git checkout <major>.<minor>.x` ) to ensure you have the proper version of the helm charts.\n  - [ ] In your terminal, change to the `./cht-core/scripts/build/helm` directory.\n  - [ ] Make sure you're using the dev EKS cluster: `kubectl config use-context arn:aws:eks:eu-west-2:720541322708:cluster/dev-cht-eks`\n  - [ ] Ensure you have access to [EKS](https://docs.communityhealthtoolkit.org/hosting/medic/) and  to the [`demo-cht` namespace](https://github.com/medic/medic-infrastructure/issues/1344).) by calling this helm command. There should be no errors: `helm list -n demo-cht`\n  - [ ] Download the current `values.yaml` data from the demo instance: `helm get values demo-cht --namespace demo-cht > values.yaml`\n  - [ ] Edit the `values.yaml` file so `cht_image_tag` and `chtversion` properties have the new tag value `<major>.<minor>.<patch>`.\n  - [ ] Use helm to upgrade the instance: `helm upgrade demo-cht . --namespace demo-cht -f values.yaml`\n  - [ ] Refresh the \"App Management\" page and verify the instance upgraded. You may need to wait 5+ minutes until the upgrade succeeds.       "body": "**Describe the bug**\nIf a user has more than 150,000 documents, `api/replication/get-ids` can fail with a 500 due to Array.push. \n\nBecause \n```\n[].push(...Array.from({ length: 130000 }).map(() => 2));\n```\n\nwill throw \n```\nUncaught RangeError: Maximum call stack size exceeded\n```\n\nSolution is never use spread push when dealing with large arrays. \n\n**To Reproduce**\n1. Launch large CHT 5.x deployment\n2. Create offline user at facility level with no replication depth\n3. Try to sync\n4. Sync errors after some time with a 500\n\n**Expected behavior**\nMaybe stopping a user with over 150,000 documents from replicating is good, but has to be intentional. \n\n**Logs**\n```\n2026-04-01T06:30:14.828 ERROR: Server error: RangeError: Maximum call stack size exceeded\n    at getDocsByReplicationKeyNouveau (/service/api/src/services/authorization.js:640:10)\n    at process.processTicksAndRejections (node:internal/process/task_queues:105:5)\n    at async Object.getContext (/service/api/src/services/replication.js:10:32)\n    at async getDocIds (/service/api/src/controllers/replication.js:7:23) {\n  [stack]: [Getter/Setter],\n  [message]: 'Maximum call stack size exceeded'\n} \n```\n\n**Environment**\n- App: api\n- Version: 5.0.x, 5.1.x\n\n**Additional context**\n<!-- Add any other context about the problem here. While this is useful we do lose visibility into individual form submissions.\n\n**We’d like to store timestamps for each form directly in the data_record document:**\n\nform_opened_at\nform_submitted_at (already mostly covered by reported_date)\n\nHaving this per-submission timing would unlock a lot of practical insights:\n\nCosting & budgeting – Understand how long each household visit actually takes\nTravel estimation – Time gaps between submissions can approximate travel between households\nQuality monitoring – Spot forms filled too quickly (possible data issues) or too slowly (training or complexity issues)\nWorkload analysis – Track CHN working hours, daily patterns, and field vs office time\n\nRight now, we’re seeing many tasks not completed so these analysis would let us deep dive on the above metrics.\n\n**Some alternatives** include\nUsing[ start and end ODK fields](https://docs.getodk.org/form-question-types/#hidden-questions) in each form , which are default ODK hidden fields that captures the timestamps.\n\n\n\n",

      },
      "body": "**Describe the bug**\nIn our api code [for sending cookies to the user](https://github.com/medic/cht-core/blob/589a9d49a6bc9f8a8af2dc38447b9265c736a5b1/api/src/services/cookie.js#L16) we have some logic for setting the [`secure` attribute](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/Security/Practical_implementation_guides/Cookies#secure).  (This attribute controls whether the cookie is only allowed to be sent via HTTPS and not just HTTP.) Unfortunately, this logic depends on the value of the `NODE_ENV` environment variable being set to `production`. Otherwise, we default to `secure: false`.  However, it seems that we are no longer setting the `NODE_ENV` value anywhere in our containers/config.  So, I do not think `secure` is ever getting set to `true` (even in production).  \n\n(It is also worth noting that we need `secure: false` when running the server locally for cht-core development since that is via HTTP.)\n\n**To Reproduce**\nDeploy a CHT server production-style (e.g. via Docker Helper). \n\nRun this curl command with your instance info:\n\n```shell\ncurl -v -k -X POST https://192-168-1-20.local-ip.medicmobile.org:37581 -H 'Content-Type: application/json' -d '{\"user\":\"medic\",\"password\":\"password\"}' 2>&1 | grep -i set-cookie\n```\n\nSee that the result is:\n\n```shell\n< set-cookie: login=force; Path=/; SameSite=Lax\n```\n\n**Expected behavior**\n\nThe result of the curl command should include `Secure;`.  Like this:\n\n```shell\n< set-cookie: login=force; Path=/; Secure; SameSite=La\n```\n\n**Additional context**\n\nThis secure cookie logic based on `NODE_ENV` was added a long time ago: https://github.com/medic/cht-core/commit/ae75e27a13730287e033542129e4f6d616a02d5b.\n\nI found this issue while reviewing [this PR](https://github.com/medic/cht-core/pull/10583) which is updating the logging to not be based on NODE_ENV.\n\n--- \n\nI am not exactly sure what the best solution here is.  We need to be able to toggle the `secure` value on for production and off for development.  I wonder if maybe we just make `NODE_ENV=production` into our [api Dockerfile](https://github.com/medic/cht-core/blob/master/api/Dockerfile) and call it good... 🤔   I suppose any time we are running in Docker, we are running with HTTPS, correct?",

      "body": "## Description\n\n`ContactChangeFilterService.isRelevantChange()` [uses](https://github.com/medic/cht-core/blob/master/webapp/src/ts/services/contact-change-filter.service.ts#L82-L86) the nullish coalescing operator (`??`) instead of logical OR (`||`):\n\n```typescript\nisRelevantChange(change, contact) {\n  return this.matchContact(change, contact) ??\n    this.isRelevantContact(change, contact) ??\n    this.isRelevantReport(change, contact);\n}\n```\n\nSince `matchContact()` always returns a boolean (`true` or `false`, never `null` or `undefined`), `false ?? expr` evaluates to `false` immediately — the `??` operator only falls through on `null`/`undefined`. This means `isRelevantContact()` and `isRelevantReport()` are never called.\n\n## Impact\nWhile testing the stock monitoring workflow we noticed a weird behavior, the summary being updated not frequently, and we were not able to know at that time, and it came out later when checking this `isRelevantChange` function:\n\nThe `user-contact-summary` cache is never invalidated when:\n- A new report is submitted for a contact (e.g., stock monitoring reports)\n- A child contact is added or modified\n\nThe cache only invalidates when the contact document itself changes (`matchContact` returns `true`).\n\nThis causes stale contact summaries in the UI until the contact doc is coincidentally modified or a full page reload occurs.\n\n### Example: Stock monitoring\n\nWhen a CHW submits a `patient_assessment_under_5` form, it creates an `sm_stock_report_chw` additional doc with `patient_id` = CHW's contact `_id`. The `isRelevantReport` method would correctly match this report via `registrationUtils.getSubjectIds`, but it is never called.\n\n**Why it \"sometimes works\":** If sentinel processing or sync touches the CHW's person doc, the cache invalidates as a side effect. But reports alone never trigger invalidation.\n\n## Fix\n\nReplace `??` with `||`:\n\n```typescript\nisRelevantChange(change, contact) {\n  return this.matchContact(change, contact) ||\n    this.isRelevantContact(change, contact) ||\n    this.isRelevantReport(change, contact);\n}\n```\n\n\ncc: @dianabarsan or @jkuester , we would need your point of view on this.",

      "body": "Depends on https://github.com/medic/cht-core/issues/10670\n\nThere are several interlocking pieces we need to add to render the UI Extensions in the webapp and handle routing to them:\n\n## UI Extensions Tab Component\n\nAdd new files: `webapp/src/ts/modules/ui-extensions/ui-extensions-tab.component.ts/html`\n\nThe HTML file needs to have the same outer framework as the other \"tab\" pages.  See the [trainings.component.html](https://github.com/medic/cht-core/blob/e33cd8738be9bbe1e3c34566fe07d7bf9fa9da6f/webapp/src/ts/modules/trainings/trainings.component.html) for example.  I think we need the `mm-tool-bar` at the top and then the `inner` and `inbox page` divs.  Then we need a custom wrapper div nested inside with the id: `ui-element-tab`.  Also , I think we can include similar `loader` logic to display a loading spinner while the extension code is being loaded.\n\nFor the `UiExtensionsTabComponent` class, we want to take the `ActivatedRoute` as a constructor parameter.  Then we can get the extension id via `route.snapshot.params['id']`.  With that id we can call the `UiExtensionsService.getExtension` method to get the actual web component code/properties.\n\nThe `UiExtensionsTabComponent` should have a property that references the wrapper div like:\n\n```ts\n@ViewChild('ui-element-tab') container!: ElementRef;`\n```\n\nFrom the `ngAfterViewInit()` method, Initialize the web component element with something like:\n\n```ts\ncustomElements.define(id, Element);\nconst element = document.createElement(id);\n// TODO Set properties on element here before appending it.\nthis.container.nativeElement.appendChild(element);\n```\n\nWe need to set the following properties:\n- `cht` - the \"CHT API\" loaded from `CHTDatasourceService.get`. Contains versioned functions for interacting with the CHT data model (from cht-datasource) as well as utility functions for doing other things (extension-libs, translate, etc)\n- `inputs` - wrapper object for all the _data_ inputs\n    - `config` - the contents of the `config` property defined in the extension properties (useful if loading custom configuration)\n    - `userContactSummary` - loaded from the `UserContactSummaryService`.\n\n## UI Extensions Tab Route Guard Provider\n\nCreate a route guard in a new file: `webapp/src/ts/modules/ui-extensions/ui-extensions-route.guard.provider.ts` -  `UiExtensionsTabRouteGuardProvider implements CanActivate`.  See the [AppRouteGuardProvider](https://github.com/medic/cht-core/blob/35662788c503441ef25ebe15ff99dbdd3bd2f104/webapp/src/ts/app-route.guard.provider.ts#L8) as an example.\n\nWhen `canActivate` is called, call  `UiExtensionsService.getProperties` method with the `route.params['id]` value to get extension properties. Fail activation if the extension does not have a `type` of `app_main_tab` or `app_drawer_tab`.\n\n## UI Extensions Routes\n\nCreate a new routes file: `webapp/src/ts/modules/ui-extensions/ui-extensions.routes.ts`. See the [training.routes.ts](https://github.com/medic/cht-core/blob/e33cd8738be9bbe1e3c34566fe07d7bf9fa9da6f/webapp/src/ts/modules/trainings/trainings.routes.ts#L8) as an example.\n\nExport a parameterized route:\n\n- `path` - `ui-extensions/:id`\n- `component` - `UiExtensionsTabComponent`\n- `canActivate` - `[UiExtensionsTabRouteGuardProvider]`\n\nUpdate `webapp/src/ts/app-routing.module.ts` to include the new route.\n\n---\n\nAdd new unit tests to the `webapp/tests/karma/ts/modules/ui-extensions` directory.",

A CI check on Dependabot PRs that runs npm install --package-lock-only and verifies the lockfile is consistent (this would flag Dependabot's broken lockfiles before merge)\n  2. A GitHub Action that auto-fixes Dependabot lockfiles by running npm install --package-lock-only and committing the result back to the PR branch\n  3. An .npmrc with optional=false to tell npm to never install optional peer deps — making both npm and Dependabot agree on the same outcome\n\nI think 3 is easiest. 1 doesn't really fix anything (still needs a human to fix the PRs). 2 is doable (claude made the action) but might be clunky?       "body": "# Planning - CHT Community \n\n- [x] Create an GH Milestone for the release and add this issue to it.\n- [x] Add all the issues to be worked on to the Milestone.\n- [x] Ensure that all issues are labelled correctly, particularly ensure that \"Regressions\" are labelled with \"Affects: <version>\" labels. The \"Affects\" label is used in a link in the Known Issues section of the release notes of that version so it has to match exactly. To make sure the label is correct go to the [release notes](https://docs.communityhealthtoolkit.org/core/releases/#release-notes) and ensure the issue is listed.\n\n# Development - Release Manager\n\nWhen development is ready to begin one of the maintainers should be nominated as a Release Manager. They will be responsible for making sure the following tasks are completed though not necessarily completing them.\n\n- [x] Set the version number in `package.json` and `package-lock.json` and submit a PR to the release branch. The easiest way to do this is to use `npm --no-git-tag-version version patch`.\n- [x] Ensure that issues from merged commits are closed and mapped to a milestone.\n- [ ] Write an update in the #stewardship-team Slack channel summarising development and identifying any blockers (the [milestone-status](https://github.com/medic/support-scripts/tree/master/milestone-status) script can be used to get a breakdown of the issues). The Release Manager is to update this every week until the version is released.\n\n# Releasing - Release Manager\n\nOnce all issues have been merged into `master` then the release process can start:\n\n- [x] Build a beta named `<major>.<minor>.<patch>-beta.1` by pushing a lightweight git tag (e.g. `git tag <major>.<minor>.<patch>-beta.1`).\n- [x] Once the CI completes successfully notify the community by creating a post titled `<major>.<minor>.<patch> Beta Releases` in the [development](https://forum.communityhealthtoolkit.org/c/development/7) category of the CHT forum using this [template](https://forum.communityhealthtoolkit.org/new-topic?title=%3Cmajor%3E.%3Cminor%3E.%3Cpatch%3E%20Beta%20Releases&body=Hi%20Everyone%0AI%E2%80%99ve%20just%20created%20the%20%60%3Cmajor%3E.%3Cminor%3E.%3Cpatch%3E-beta.1%60%20tag.%0APlease%20let%20me%20know%20if%20there%E2%80%99s%20any%20final%20update%20we%20need%20to%20make.%0AIf%20all%20is%20good%2C%20then%20in%2024h%2C%20I%20will%20start%20the%20release.%20Thanks%21&category=development).\n- [x] Add release notes to the [Core Framework Releases](https://docs.communityhealthtoolkit.org/core/releases/) page:\n  - [x] Create a new document for the release in the [releases folder](https://github.com/medic/cht-docs/tree/main/content/en/core/releases).\n  - [x] Ensure all issues are in the GH Milestone, they have human readable descriptions, and that they're correctly labelled. In particular: they have one \"Type\" label, \"UI/UX\" if they change the UI, and \"Breaking change\" if appropriate.\n  - [x] Use [this script](https://github.com/medic/cht-core/blob/master/scripts/release-notes/index.js) to export the issues into our release note format.\n  - [x] Collect known migration steps, descriptions, screenshots, videos, data, and anything else to help communicate particularly important changes. This information should already be on the issue, but if not, prompt the change author to provide it.\n  - [x] Document any required or recommended upgrades to our other products (eg: cht-conf, cht-gateway, cht-android).\n  - [x] Ensure that the release notes PR is merged before moving to next step.\n- [x] Create a [new release](https://github.com/medic/cht-core/releases/new) in GitHub, with the naming convention `<major>.<minor>.<patch>`, from the release branch created above as the target branch. Click on the \"Choose a tag\" dropdown and create a tag for the release with the naming convention `<major>.<minor>.<patch>`. Add a link to the release notes page in the description of the release.\n- [x] Once you publish the release, confirm the release build completes successfully and the new release is available on the [market](https://staging.dev.medicmobile.org/_couch/builds_4/_design/builds/_view/releases). Make sure that the document has new entry with `id: medic:medic:<major>.<minor>.<patch>`\n- [x] Upgrade the [demo](https://demo-cht.dev.medicmobile.org/) instance to the newly released version.\n- [x] Announce the release on the [CHT Forum](https://forum.communityhealthtoolkit.org/), under the \"Announcements - Releases\" category using this [template](https://forum.communityhealthtoolkit.org/new-topic?title=Announcing%20the%20release%20of%20%3Cmajor%3E.%3Cminor%3E.%3Cpatch%3E%20of%20the%20CHT%20Core%20Framework&body=%2AAnnouncing%20the%20release%20of%20%7B%7Bversion%7D%7D%20of%20%7B%7Bproduct%7D%7D%2A%0AThis%20release%20fixes%20%7B%7Bnumber%20of%20bugs%7D%7D.%20Read%20the%20%5Brelease%20notes%5D%28%7B%7Burl%7D%7D%29%20for%20full%20details.&category=releases).\n- [x] Go over the list of commits and individually notify contributing / interested community members about the release.\n- [x] Go to the [Issues tab](https://github.com/medic/cht-core/issues) and filter the issues with `is:issue label:\"Affects: 4.x.x\" ` , replace `4.x.x` with the previous version number. Add any open \"known issues\" from the prior release that were not fixed in this release. Done by adding the correct `Affects: 4.x.x` label.\n- [x] Mark this issue \"done\" and close the Milestone.\n",
